<h2 id="usage" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Usage<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#usage"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>Import the steps package:</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword module">import</span> <span class="token imports"><span class="token operator">*</span> <span class="token keyword module">as</span> steps</span> <span class="token keyword module">from</span> <span class="token string">&quot;@zag-js/steps&quot;</span>
</span></div></pre>
<p>The steps package exports two key functions:</p>
<ul>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">machine</code> - State machine logic.</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">connect</code> - Maps machine state to JSX props and event handlers.</li>
</ul>
<p>Then use the framework integration helpers:</p>

<h2 id="setting-the-initial-step" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Setting the initial step<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#setting-the-initial-step"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>Set the initial step by passing <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">defaultStep</code> to the machine context.</p>
<blockquote class="my_5 px_4 py_3 bg_bg.tertiary.subtle bd-w_1px bd-l-c_border.primary.subtle bd-l-w_2px bdr_4px bd-c_border">
<p>The value of the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">step</code> property is zero-based index.</p>
</blockquote>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>steps<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">defaultStep</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">1</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h2 id="controlled-current-step" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Controlled current step<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#controlled-current-step"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>Use <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">step</code> and <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onStepChange</code> for controlled usage.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>steps<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  step<span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token function">onStepChange</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">details</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token function">setStep</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>details<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">step</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h2 id="listening-for-step-change" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Listening for step change<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#listening-for-step-change"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>When the active step changes, the machine will invoke the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onStepChange</code> event</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>steps<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token function">onStepChange</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">details</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">    <span class="token comment">// details =&gt; { step: number }</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">    <span class="token console class-name">console</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token template-string"><span class="token template-punctuation string">`</span><span class="token string">Step changed to </span><span class="token interpolation"><span class="token interpolation-punctuation punctuation">${</span>details<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">step</span><span class="token interpolation-punctuation punctuation">}</span></span><span class="token template-punctuation string">`</span></span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h2 id="listening-for-steps-completion" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Listening for steps completion<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#listening-for-steps-completion"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>When all steps are completed, the machine will invoke the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onStepComplete</code> event</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>steps<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>

</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h2 id="enforcing-linear-steps" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Enforcing linear steps<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#enforcing-linear-steps"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>To enforce linear steps, you can set the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">linear</code> prop to <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">true</code> when creating
the steps machine. This will prevent users from skipping steps.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>steps<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">linear</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token boolean">true</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h2 id="validating-steps-in-linear-mode" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Validating steps in linear mode<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#validating-steps-in-linear-mode"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>Use <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">isStepValid</code> to block forward navigation when a step is incomplete.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>steps<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>

</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token comment">// details =&gt; { step: number, action: &quot;next&quot; | &quot;set&quot;, targetStep?: number }</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token console class-name">console</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;blocked at step&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> details<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">step</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h2 id="skipping-optional-steps" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Skipping optional steps<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#skipping-optional-steps"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>Use <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">isStepSkippable</code> when some steps should be bypassed by next/prev
navigation.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>steps<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>

</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h2 id="changing-the-orientation" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Changing the orientation<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#changing-the-orientation"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>The steps machine supports both horizontal and vertical orientations. You can
set the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">orientation</code> prop to <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">horizontal</code> or <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">vertical</code> to change the
orientation of the steps.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>steps<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">orientation</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;vertical&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h2 id="programmatic-navigation" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Programmatic navigation<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#programmatic-navigation"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>Use the API methods to move through the flow in code.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line">api<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">setStep</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">2</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>

<h2 id="styling-guide" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Styling guide<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#styling-guide"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>Each part includes a <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-part</code> attribute you can target in CSS.</p>
<pre class="prose language-css"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-scope</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;steps&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;root&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>

</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-scope</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;steps&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;root&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-orientation</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;horizontal|vertical&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>

</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-scope</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;steps&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;list&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for the list part */</span>

</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-scope</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;steps&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;list&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-orientation</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;horizontal|vertical&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>

</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-scope</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;steps&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;separator&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>

<h3 id="current-step" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Current step<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#current-step"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>To style the current step, you can use the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-current</code> attribute.</p>
<pre class="prose language-css"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-scope</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;steps&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;item&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-current</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* item styles for the current step */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">

<h2 id="methods-and-properties" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Methods and Properties<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#methods-and-properties"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<h3 id="machine-context" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Machine Context<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#machine-context"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>The steps machine exposes the following context properties:</p>
<ul class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 pl_0! li-t_none dvd-y_1px li-pos_inside"><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">ids</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">ElementIds</code><span class="d_block">The custom ids for the stepper elements</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">step</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">number</code><span class="d_block">The controlled value of the stepper</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">defaultStep</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">number</code><span class="d_block">The initial value of the stepper when rendered.
Use when you don&#x27;t need to control the value of the stepper.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onStepChange</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(details: StepChangeDetails) =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">Callback to be called when the value changes</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onStepComplete</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">VoidFunction</code><span class="d_block">Callback to be called when a step is completed</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">linear</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">If `true`, the stepper requires the user to complete the steps in order</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">orientation</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">&quot;horizontal&quot; | &quot;vertical&quot;</code><span class="d_block">The orientation of the stepper</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">count</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">number</code><span class="d_block">The total number of steps</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">isStepValid</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(index: number) =&gt; boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether a step is valid. Invalid steps block forward navigation in linear mode.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">isStepSkippable</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(index: number) =&gt; boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether a step can be skipped during navigation.
Skippable steps are bypassed when using next/prev.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onStepInvalid</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(details: StepInvalidDetails) =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">Called when navigation is blocked due to an invalid step.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">dir</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">&quot;ltr&quot; | &quot;rtl&quot;</code><span class="d_block">The document&#x27;s text/writing direction.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">id</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">string</code><span class="d_block">The unique identifier of the machine.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">getRootNode</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">() =&gt; ShadowRoot | Node | Document</code><span class="d_block">A root node to correctly resolve document in custom environments. E.x.: Iframes, Electron.</span></li></ul>
<h3 id="machine-api" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Machine API<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#machine-api"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>The steps <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">api</code> exposes the following methods:</p>
<ul class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 pl_0! li-t_none dvd-y_1px li-pos_inside"><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px stepper.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">number</code><span class="d_block">The total number of steps.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap class="d_block">Whether the stepper has a next step.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em prose">isStepValid</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(index: number) =&gt; boolean</code><span class="d_block">Check if a specific step is valid (lazy evaluation)</span></li><li prose">isStepSkippable</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(index: number) =&gt; boolean</code><span class="d_block">Check if a specific step can be skipped</span></li><li class="d_flex process.\n\n\u003cResources pkg=\"@zag-js/steps\" /\u003e\n\n\u003cShowcase id=\"Steps\" /\u003e\n\n**Features**\n\n- Supports horizontal and vertical orientations\n- Supports changing the active step with the keyboard and pointer\n- Supports linear and non-linear steps\n\n## Installation\n\nInstall the steps package:\n\n\u003cCodeSnippet id=\"steps/installation.mdx\" /\u003e\n\n## Anatomy\n\nCheck the steps anatomy and part names.\n\n\u003e Each part includes a `data-part` attribute to help identify them in the DOM.\n\n\u003cAnatomy id=\"steps\" /\u003e\n\n## Usage\n\nImport the steps package:\n\n```jsx\nimport * as steps from \"@zag-js/steps\"\n```\n\nThe steps package exports two key functions:\n\n- `machine` - State machine logic.\n- `connect` - Maps machine state to JSX props and event handlers.\n\nThen use the framework integration helpers:\n\n\u003cCodeSnippet id=\"steps/usage.mdx\" /\u003e\n\n## Setting the initial step\n\nSet the initial step by passing `defaultStep` to the machine context.\n\n\u003e The value of the `step` property is zero-based index.\n\n```jsx {2}\nconst service = useMachine(steps.machine, {\n  defaultStep: 1,\n})\n```\n\n## Controlled current step\n\nUse `step` and `onStepChange` for controlled usage.\n\n```jsx\nconst service = useMachine(steps.machine, {\n  step,\n  onStepChange(details) {\n    setStep(details.step)\n  },\n})\n```\n\n## Listening for step change\n\nWhen the active step changes, the machine will invoke the `onStepChange` event\n\n```jsx {2-4}\nconst service = useMachine(steps.machine, {\n  onStepChange(details) {\n    // details =\u003e { step: number }\n    console.log(`Step changed to ${details.step}`)\n  },\n})\n```\n\n## Listening for steps completion\n\nWhen all steps are completed, the machine will invoke the `onStepComplete` event\n\n```jsx {2-4}\nconst service = useMachine(steps.machine, {\n  onStepComplete() {\n    console.log(\"All steps are complete\")\n  },\n})\n```\n\n## Enforcing linear steps\n\nTo enforce linear steps, you can set the `linear` prop to `true` when creating\nthe steps machine. This will prevent users from skipping steps.\n\n```jsx {2}\nconst service = useMachine(steps.machine, {\n  linear: true,\n})\n```\n\n## Validating steps in linear mode\n\nUse `isStepValid` to block forward navigation when a step is incomplete.\n\n```jsx\nconst service = useMachine(steps.machine, {\n  linear: true,\n  isStepValid(index) {\n    return completedSteps.has(index)\n  },\n  onStepInvalid(details) {\n    // details =\u003e { step: number, action: \"next\" | \"set\", targetStep?: number }\n    console.log(\"blocked at step\", details.step)\n  },\n})\n```\n\n## Skipping optional steps\n\nUse `isStepSkippable` when some steps should be bypassed by next/prev\nnavigation.\n\n```jsx\nconst service = useMachine(steps.machine, {\n  isStepSkippable(index) {\n    return index === 2\n  },\n})\n```\n\n## Changing the orientation\n\nThe steps machine supports both horizontal and vertical orientations. You can\nset the `orientation` prop to `horizontal` or `vertical` to change the\norientation of the steps.\n\n```jsx {2}\nconst service = useMachine(steps.machine, {\n  orientation: \"vertical\",\n})\n```\n\n## Programmatic navigation\n\nUse the API methods to move through the flow in code.\n\n```jsx\napi.setStep(2)\napi.goToNextStep()\napi.goToPrevStep()\napi.resetStep()\n```\n\n## Styling guide\n\nEach part includes a `data-part` attribute you can target in CSS.\n\n```css\n[data-scope=\"steps\"][data-part=\"root\"] {\n  /* styles for the root part */\n}\n\n[data-scope=\"steps\"][data-part=\"root\"][data-orientation=\"horizontal|vertical\"] {\n  /* styles for the root part based on orientation */\n}\n\n[data-scope=\"steps\"][data-part=\"list\"] {\n  /* styles for the list part */\n}\n\n[data-scope=\"steps\"][data-part=\"list\"][data-orientation=\"horizontal|vertical\"] {\n  /* styles for the list part based on orientation */\n}\n\n[data-scope=\"steps\"][data-part=\"separator\"] {\n  /* styles for the separator part */\n}\n\n[data-scope=\"steps\"][data-part=\"separator\"][data-orientation=\"horizontal|vertical\"] {\n  /* styles for the separator part based on orientation */\n}\n```\n\n### Current step\n\nTo style the current step, you can use the `data-current` attribute.\n\n```css\n[data-scope=\"steps\"][data-part=\"item\"][data-current] {\n  /* item styles for the current step */\n}\n\n[data-scope=\"steps\"][data-part=\"separator\"][data-current] {\n  /* separator styles for the current step */\n}\n```\n\n### Completed step\n\nTo style the completed step, you can use the `data-complete` attribute.\n\n```css\n[data-scope=\"steps\"][data-part=\"item\"][data-complete] {\n  /* item styles for the completed step */\n}\n\n[data-scope=\"steps\"][data-part=\"separator\"][data-complete] {\n  /* separator styles for the completed step */\n}\n```\n\n### Incomplete step\n\nTo style the incomplete step, you can use the `data-incomplete` attribute.\n\n```css\n[data-scope=\"steps\"][data-part=\"item\"][data-incomplete] {\n  /* item styles for the incomplete step */\n}\n\n[data-scope=\"steps\"][data-part=\"separator\"][data-incomplete] {\n  /* separator styles for the incomplete step */\n}\n```\n\n## Methods and Properties\n\n### Machine Context\n\nThe steps machine exposes the following context properties:\n\n\u003cContextTable name=\"steps\" /\u003e\n\n### Machine API\n\nThe steps `api` exposes the following methods:\n\n\u003cApiTable name=\"steps\" /\u003e\n\n### Data Attributes\n\n\u003cDataAttrTable name=\"steps\" /\u003e\n\n### CSS Variables\n\n\u003cCssVarTable name=\"steps\" /\u003e"])</script><script>self.__next_f.push([1,"5:[\"$\",\"$Le\",null,{\"doc\":{\"title\":\"Steps\",\"description\":\"Using the steps
